### Original Query ###
PREFIX schema: <https://schema.org/>
PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#>
SELECT (COUNT(*) AS ?count) WHERE {
  ?person a schema:Person .
  ?person schema:memberOf ?org .
  ?org schema:department ?department .
  ?department schema:makesOffer ?offer .
  ?offer schema:itemOffered ?work .
  ?work schema:about ?topic .
  ?topic schema:mainEntityOfPage ?page .
  OPTIONAL {
    {
      ?work schema:position ?optRank .
      FILTER(?optRank IN (1, 2, 3))
    }
    UNION
    {
      ?page schema:position ?optRank .
      FILTER(?optRank IN (7, 8, 9))
    }
  }
  OPTIONAL { ?person schema:award ?optAward . }
}

         Count

SELECT (COUNT(*) AS ?count) WHERE {
  ?org <https://schema.org/department> ?department .
  ?department <https://schema.org/makesOffer> ?offer .
  ?offer <https://schema.org/itemOffered> ?work .
  ?work <https://schema.org/about> ?topic .
  ?person <https://schema.org/memberOf> ?org .
  ?topic <https://schema.org/mainEntityOfPage> ?page .
  ?person a <https://schema.org/Person> .
  OPTIONAL {
    {
      ?work <https://schema.org/position> ?optRank .
      FILTER (?optRank IN (1, 2, 3))
    }
    UNION
    {
      ?page <https://schema.org/position> ?optRank .
      FILTER (?optRank IN (7, 8, 9))
    }
  }
  OPTIONAL {
    ?person <https://schema.org/award> ?optAward .
  }
}

         Count

SELECT (COUNT(*) AS ?count) WHERE {
  ?org <https://schema.org/department> ?department .
  ?department <https://schema.org/makesOffer> ?offer .
  ?offer <https://schema.org/itemOffered> ?work .
  ?work <https://schema.org/about> ?topic .
  ?person <https://schema.org/memberOf> ?org .
  ?topic <https://schema.org/mainEntityOfPage> ?page .
  ?person a <https://schema.org/Person> .
  OPTIONAL {
    {
      ?work <https://schema.org/position> ?optRank .
      FILTER (?optRank IN (1, 2, 3))
    }
    UNION
    {
      ?page <https://schema.org/position> ?optRank .
      FILTER (?optRank IN (7, 8, 9))
    }
  }
  OPTIONAL {
    ?person <https://schema.org/award> ?optAward .
  }
}

         Count (hasNextFalseCountActual=0)

SELECT (COUNT(*) AS ?count) WHERE {
  ?org <https://schema.org/department> ?department .
  ?department <https://schema.org/makesOffer> ?offer .
  ?offer <https://schema.org/itemOffered> ?work .
  ?work <https://schema.org/about> ?topic .
  ?person <https://schema.org/memberOf> ?org .
  ?topic <https://schema.org/mainEntityOfPage> ?page .
  ?person a <https://schema.org/Person> .
  OPTIONAL {
    {
      ?work <https://schema.org/position> ?optRank .
      FILTER (?optRank IN (1, 2, 3))
    }
    UNION
    {
      ?page <https://schema.org/position> ?optRank .
      FILTER (?optRank IN (7, 8, 9))
    }
  }
  OPTIONAL {
    ?person <https://schema.org/award> ?optAward .
  }
}

2285.364 ms/op

### Original Query ###
PREFIX schema: <https://schema.org/>
PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#>
SELECT (COUNT(DISTINCT ?person) AS ?count) WHERE {
  ?person a schema:Person .
  ?person schema:memberOf ?org .
  ?org schema:department ?department .
  ?department schema:makesOffer ?offer .
  ?offer schema:itemOffered ?work .
  ?work schema:about ?topic .
  ?topic schema:mainEntityOfPage ?page .
  OPTIONAL {
    ?person schema:award ?optAward .
  }
  FILTER(?optAward != "")
  BIND(?optAward AS ?awardBinding)
  OPTIONAL { ?work schema:review ?review . }
}

SELECT (COUNT(DISTINCT ?person) AS ?count) WHERE {
  ?person <https://schema.org/memberOf> ?org .
  ?person a <https://schema.org/Person> .
  ?org <https://schema.org/department> ?department .
  ?department <https://schema.org/makesOffer> ?offer .
  ?offer <https://schema.org/itemOffered> ?work .
  ?work <https://schema.org/about> ?topic .
  ?topic <https://schema.org/mainEntityOfPage> ?page .
  ?person <https://schema.org/award> ?optAward .
  FILTER (?optAward != "")
  BIND(?optAward AS ?awardBinding)
  OPTIONAL {
    ?work <https://schema.org/review> ?review .
  }
}

   │  ╚══ GroupElem (count)
   │        Count (Distinct)
   │           Var (name=person) (bindingState=bound)
   └── ExtensionElem (count)
         Count (Distinct)
            Var (name=person) (bindingState=unbound)

SELECT (COUNT(DISTINCT ?person) AS ?count) WHERE {
  ?person <https://schema.org/memberOf> ?org .
  ?person a <https://schema.org/Person> .
  ?org <https://schema.org/department> ?department .
  ?department <https://schema.org/makesOffer> ?offer .
  ?offer <https://schema.org/itemOffered> ?work .
  ?work <https://schema.org/about> ?topic .
  ?topic <https://schema.org/mainEntityOfPage> ?page .
  ?person <https://schema.org/award> ?optAward .
  FILTER (?optAward != "")
  BIND(?optAward AS ?awardBinding)
  OPTIONAL {
    ?work <https://schema.org/review> ?review .
  }
}

SELECT (COUNT(DISTINCT ?person) AS ?count) WHERE {
  ?person <https://schema.org/memberOf> ?org .
  ?person a <https://schema.org/Person> .
  ?org <https://schema.org/department> ?department .
  ?department <https://schema.org/makesOffer> ?offer .
  ?offer <https://schema.org/itemOffered> ?work .
  ?work <https://schema.org/about> ?topic .
  ?topic <https://schema.org/mainEntityOfPage> ?page .
  ?person <https://schema.org/award> ?optAward .
  FILTER (?optAward != "")
  BIND(?optAward AS ?awardBinding)
  OPTIONAL {
    ?work <https://schema.org/review> ?review .
  }
}

### Original Query ###
PREFIX schema: <https://schema.org/>
PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#>
SELECT (COUNT(*) AS ?count) WHERE {
  ?person a schema:Person .
  ?person schema:memberOf ?org .
  ?org schema:department ?department .
  ?department schema:makesOffer ?offer .
  ?offer schema:itemOffered ?work .
  ?work schema:about ?topic .
  ?topic schema:mainEntityOfPage ?page .
  OPTIONAL {
    ?page schema:event ?event .
    ?event schema:position ?eventPosition .
    FILTER(?eventPosition IN (1, 2, 3, 4))
    BIND(?eventPosition AS ?eventBucket)
  }
  OPTIONAL { ?org schema:employee ?optEmployee . }
}

SELECT (COUNT(*) AS ?count) WHERE {
  ?org <https://schema.org/department> ?department .
  ?department <https://schema.org/makesOffer> ?offer .
  ?offer <https://schema.org/itemOffered> ?work .
  ?work <https://schema.org/about> ?topic .
  ?person <https://schema.org/memberOf> ?org .
  ?topic <https://schema.org/mainEntityOfPage> ?page .
  ?person a <https://schema.org/Person> .
  OPTIONAL {
    VALUES ?eventPosition { "1"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "2"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "3"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "4"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> }
    ?event <https://schema.org/position> ?eventPosition .
    ?page <https://schema.org/event> ?event .
    BIND(?eventPosition AS ?eventBucket)
  }
  OPTIONAL {
    ?org <https://schema.org/employee> ?optEmployee .
  }
}

PREFIX schema: <https://schema.org/>
PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#>
SELECT (COUNT(*) AS ?count) WHERE {
  ?person a schema:Person .
  ?person schema:memberOf ?org .
  ?org schema:department ?department .
  ?department schema:makesOffer ?offer .
  ?offer schema:itemOffered ?work .
  ?work schema:about ?topic .
  ?topic schema:mainEntityOfPage ?page .
  OPTIONAL {
    {
      ?work schema:review ?shared .
    }
    UNION
    {
      ?page schema:event ?shared .
    }
    OPTIONAL { ?shared a ?sharedType . }
  }
  ?person schema:identifier ?personIdentifier .
  FILTER(?personIdentifier IN (1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7))
}

SELECT (COUNT(*) AS ?count) WHERE {
  VALUES ?personIdentifier { "1"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "2"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "3"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "4"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "5"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "6"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "7"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> }
  ?person <https://schema.org/identifier> ?personIdentifier .
  ?person a <https://schema.org/Person> .
  ?person <https://schema.org/memberOf> ?org .
  ?org <https://schema.org/department> ?department .
  ?department <https://schema.org/makesOffer> ?offer .
  ?offer <https://schema.org/itemOffered> ?work .
  ?work <https://schema.org/about> ?topic .
  ?topic <https://schema.org/mainEntityOfPage> ?page .
  OPTIONAL {
    {
      ?work <https://schema.org/review> ?shared .
      OPTIONAL {
        ?shared a ?sharedType .
      }
    }
    UNION
    {
      ?page <https://schema.org/event> ?shared .
      OPTIONAL {
        ?shared a ?sharedType .
      }
    }
  }
}

SELECT (COUNT(*) AS ?count) WHERE {
  VALUES ?personIdentifier { "1"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "2"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "3"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "4"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "5"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "6"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "7"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> }
  ?person <https://schema.org/identifier> ?personIdentifier .
  ?person a <https://schema.org/Person> .
  ?person <https://schema.org/memberOf> ?org .
  ?org <https://schema.org/department> ?department .
  ?department <https://schema.org/makesOffer> ?offer .
  ?offer <https://schema.org/itemOffered> ?work .
  ?work <https://schema.org/about> ?topic .
  ?topic <https://schema.org/mainEntityOfPage> ?page .
  OPTIONAL {
    {
      ?work <https://schema.org/review> ?shared .
      OPTIONAL {
        ?shared a ?sharedType .
      }
    }
    UNION
    {
      ?page <https://schema.org/event> ?shared .
      OPTIONAL {
        ?shared a ?sharedType .
      }
    }
  }
}

SELECT (COUNT(*) AS ?count) WHERE {
  VALUES ?personIdentifier { "1"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "2"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "3"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "4"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "5"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "6"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> "7"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int> }
  ?person <https://schema.org/identifier> ?personIdentifier .
  ?person a <https://schema.org/Person> .
  ?person <https://schema.org/memberOf> ?org .
  ?org <https://schema.org/department> ?department .
  ?department <https://schema.org/makesOffer> ?offer .
  ?offer <https://schema.org/itemOffered> ?work .
  ?work <https://schema.org/about> ?topic .
  ?topic <https://schema.org/mainEntityOfPage> ?page .
  OPTIONAL {
    {
      ?work <https://schema.org/review> ?shared .
      OPTIONAL {
        ?shared a ?sharedType .
      }
    }
    UNION
    {
      ?page <https://schema.org/event> ?shared .
      OPTIONAL {
        ?shared a ?sharedType .
      }
    }
  }
}

228.118 ms/op
